 karnataka vidhansabha ne jane-maane patrkaar ravi belagere samet do kannada tabloid ke sampadakon ko rajya ke vidhayakon ke khilaaf kathith manahanikaarak lekh likhakar visheshadhikaar hanan karne ke liye unhen ek saal ke karawas kii sajaa sunai he
 The speakers of the meeting held in the press club felt that the jail sentence in cases like defamation is misuse of the privileges of the assembly
 vidhayakon ke liye uchit yah hota ki agar unhen laga ki wo aalekh manahanikaarak hai, to wo un patrakaron ke khilaaf naagarik manahani kaa cese darj kara sakate the
 Seema Mustafa, editor-in-chief of 'the Citizen' said, 'disagreement is something that governments with authoritarian tendencies have always targeted
 ' unhone media se iskaa ehsaas karne kii baat kehete hue kaha, 'hamaari takat un logon se aati he jinaki or jinke liye ham aawaaj uthaate hai, na ki prabandhan yaa sarkaar se
 ' da vir ke founding editor siddharth varadarajan ne kaha, 'pakistan kii jeet ke baad pataakhe jalaane ko lekar giraftaar ho rahi he, yah is baat kaa sanket he ki loktantr kis disha main ja rahaa he
 ' lekin keval sarkaar yaa rajya kii mashinari hi nahin hai jo patrakaron ko nishaanaa bana rahe hai

 vah us vimugdh karne vaali milawat main apane kala-aswaad kaa aishwarya ganvaata he, jise ek shaayar or gayika ne milakar rachaa he
 
 
 
 or jiske sammohan se ab umr bhar begum akhtar or shakeel badayunni batch nahin sakate, chaahakar nikal bhi nahin sakate
 In the era of Akhtaribai Faizabadi that we are remembering today, it becomes very important to mark one of the customs of the music world at that time
 tawaayphen or baiyaan rajdarbaron main yaa khud ke kothon par mehfilein do tareekon se sajaati thim- ‘baithki mehfil’ tathaa ‘khadi mehfil’
 'sitki Mahfil' was more popular, because in it the singer performed the soulful performances of Thumri, Dadra, Sadra, Holi and Ghazals etc
 baiyon kaa baari kapadaa or shringaar aam logon ke aakarshan kaa kendra hua karata tha, jise peshwaz kehete hai
 The 'khadi mahafil' was seldom, in which the singer would pay the songs while standing with little limb movement
 ek prakaar se ise ham mujre kaa hi prakaar kah sakate hai
 The accompaniments followed the singer, sometimes even running
 kab ‘sam’ aayega, kab ‘theka’ lenaa he- iskaa khaas khyaal rakhte the
 Tablabas' tabla used to hang tight in their waist
 gayika gum-ghumkar mehfil main apane fan kaa rang bikherti thi
 Book: Akhtari: Afzal of Soz and Saaz Editor: Yatindra Mishra Prakashkar: Vani Prakashan, New Delhi Page No: 276 Price: Rs

 In a program in Hingoli, Maharashtra, Home Minister Sushil Kumar Shinde said that he had to cancel the holidays of many policemen due to a 'freak' chief minister's dharna
 gauratlab he ki dilli ke mukhyamantri arvind kejariwal rail bhawan ke kareeb do din tak dharne par baithe the

 kejariwal kii maang kathith laaparvaahee baratane vaale police waalon ko nilambit karne kii thi

 vartmaan main dilli police kendriya grahamantri ko report karti he
 The Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) is in full action mode for the by-election for 12 assembly seats in Uttar Pradesh
 11 siton par jahaan ek-ek mantri ko lagaaya gaya he, vahiin haari hui seat jalalpur jeetne ke liye do mantriyon kii tainaati kii gai he
 At present, the BJP is busy finalizing the names of the winning candidates
 isko lekar mukhyamantri yogi adityanath ke paanch kalidaas maarg sthit sarkari awaas par kor group kii baithak bhi ho chuki he
 In which BJP state president Dr
 mahendra nath pandeya, sanghathan mahaamantri sunil bansal jitau oommidavaaron par charchaa kar chuke hai
 Party sources say that after becoming MP, some party mlas want to get tickets from their seats to their relatives, but the party is in a mood to replace their relatives with militant activists working for the organization
 sifarish ke aadhaar par party kisi kamjor ummidavaar ko utaarne kaa khatra mol nahin legi
 BJP vacated all the assembly seats- Cantt (lucknow), Zaidpur (barabanki), Manikpur (chitrakoot), Gangoh (saharanpur), Iglas (aligarh), Rampur, Tundla (firozabad), Govindnagar (kanpur), Balha (bahraich), In order to win Pratapgarh, Jalalpur (ambedkaranagar), Hamirpur has started preparing the array
 is baar ke loksabhaa chunaav main jeetne vaale yogi sarkaar main mantri rahe satyadev pachori, reeta bahuguna joshi or espi singh baghel kii siten bhi khaali hui hai
 In the 12 assembly seats which are to be held vacant due to mlas winning the Lok Sabha elections, BJP has ten seats in it
 2017 ke vidhansabha chunaav main rampur se sapa pratyaashee ajam khan or jalalpur vidhansabha seat par basapa pratyaashee reetesh pandeya prachand modi lahar ke baavjood jite the
 In such a situation, the BJP has made a special plan to capture both these seats in the by-elections
 haari hui rampur seat jeetne ke liye bijepi ne up mukhyamantri dinesh sharma ko jimmedaari saunpi he, vahiin jalalpur (ambedkarnagar) seat jeetne ke liye do-do mantriyon ko jimmaa saunpa he
 Minister Brajesh Pathak and Santosh Singh will be responsible for winning the Jalalpur seat
 jabaki anya 10 siton ke liye ek-ek mantri lagaae gaye hai
 Deputy CM Keshav Maurya has been given to Govindnagar, Minister Shrikant Sharma to Tundla, Ashutosh Tandon to Lucknow Cantt, Dara Singh Chauhan to Zaidpur, Ramapati Shastri to Balha, and Pratapgarh to Transport Minister Swatantra Dev Singh
 isi tarah mahendra singh ko manikpur, bhupendra singh ko gangoh, dhunni singh ko hamirpur jitaane ke liye bijepi ne lagaaya he
